5:23:57 world number three user control and

5:24:15 number four

5:24:52 number six recognition rather than

7:29:04 there but the development of the project
7:29:06 is completed

7:30:10 as possible this way ideas can be tested

7:30:20 never really done instead there is an
7:30:23 ever evolving process that includes
7:30:25 cycles of user experience design
7:30:27 development testing and launch in

9:48:35 why peer review is important to a
9:48:38 creative practice
9:48:40 design is rarely a solitary practice
9:48:43 as a designer you might be working with
9:48:45 clients or have a boss you need to
9:48:47 report to you might also be part of a
9:48:49 design team or even managing a team of
9:48:52 your own
9:48:53 you might be asked to present a project
9:48:55 to stakeholders at a company or pitch
9:48:57 your services to a new client
9:49:00 ultimately your design needs to stand
9:49:02 alone but in the process of making
9:49:04 design you should be testing out your
9:49:06 ideas with an audience getting feedback
9:49:09 and developing your design accordingly
9:49:12 design is very intertwined with
9:49:14 communication
9:49:15 and to be a successful designer you need
9:49:18 to be able to talk about your work to
9:49:20 explain it and show that you understand
9:49:23 how it's working
9:49:25 in different situations it may be
9:49:27 necessary to explain your own work and

9:49:31 constructive way
9:49:34 so in this course you'll be engaging in

9:49:48 practice

9:49:51 observe and openly reflect on what is
